## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0002 [0x2F] EventEntity->Render.Flags0 &= ~0x80000 // Bit 19
  1: 0x0008 [0x37] UPDATE_EVENT_POSITION_AND_DIR: x=-409.174*, z=121.642*, y=0.499*, direction=166.7*
  2: 0x0011 [0x22] ENTITY_HIDE_FLAG(enabled=0x00)
  3: 0x0013 [0x80] LOAD_WAIT(entity=EventEntity)
  4: 0x0018 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
